In addition, there are three others, including Tan Fulie, who are already studying at Japanese vocational schools or auditing courses at the Army University in advance.

Hu Ruoyu Discusses Governance Policies for Qingdao

Qingdao dispatch: The newly appointed Mayor of Qingdao, Hu Ruoyu, arrived in Qingdao on the morning of the 1st. After resting at the mayor's official residence, he moved into the International Sanitarium. I visited him at half past two in the afternoon. He was napping, so I waited in the reception room, where several others were already waiting. At three o'clock, Hu came out to meet us, wearing a white Zhongshan suit, very plainly dressed. After the greetings, I asked, "How long was your journey here, Mayor?" Hu replied, "I left Beidaihe at noon on the 30th of last month and arrived in Qingdao at ten o'clock this morning, so it was only forty-eight hours on the way." I asked, "When will you take office?" He answered, "Mayor Ge has already left Qingdao, and the municipal government cannot be without someone in charge. I intended to take office today, but Mr. Cai (Yuanpei) has not returned from his visit to Laoshan, and there are still matters to discuss with him. Therefore, I have set the 4th as the day to take over and have invited Mr. Cai to represent the supervisor of the oath nearby." I asked, "What are your policies after taking office?" He replied, "I am not very familiar with the situation in Qingdao. Future policies will require me to observe the local circumstances to formulate specific plans. However, my mission here is to work, not just to be an official. In my opinion, Qingdao, being a place of international attention, should have minimal contact with political affairs and focus on developing industry and commerce, making it a commercialized city. Qingdao is the only commercial port in North China with numerous factories. If we expand upon its existing advantages, the development of industry and commerce would be limitless. To develop commerce, we must first ensure that capitalists are willing to invest. Therefore, maintaining public order is of utmost importance. After taking office, I will do everything in my power to maintain the city's security, so that it is not affected by the domestic turmoil, and the citizens can live and work in peace. Capitalists will naturally come to Qingdao upon hearing of this, and the commercial situation is expected to improve. Furthermore, education in this city is very backward, with too many out-of-school children. Those residing in Qingdao often have no choice but to move elsewhere because their children have no place to study, which is a negative phenomenon. In the future, we must strive to develop education to make it a cultural center. In addition, for municipal administration, we must undertake projects that benefit the citizens and eliminate what the citizens detest. I hope the press will provide guidance at any time." I asked, "Is it true, as reported, that Zhang Xueming will be the commander of the Qingdao garrison?" He replied, "This is a rumor fabricated by a Japanese newspaper; there is absolutely no such thing." I asked, "Where are Mr. Li Shizeng and Commander Shen now?" He answered, "Mr. Li is in Beidaihe, and Commander Shen returned to Shenyang with Commander Zhang on the morning of the 30th to inspect the Jiang defenses and then return to Qingdao." I asked, "What is Commander Zhang's attitude towards the current situation?" He replied, "Commander Zhang has always advocated peaceful reunification." At this point, due to the presence of other guests, I took my leave. (September 1st)

The Scourge of War in Chenliu and Tongxu

Kaifeng dispatch: A friend who returned from the war zone, passing through Chenliu and Tongxu, witnessed the devastation of the war. According to him, Chenliu, located at a crossroads, is the gateway to eastern Henan. As the rear of the war, it has suffered from years of bandits, floods, droughts, and famines. This year, the massive concentration of troops for several months has caused even greater losses. According to locals, they were required to supply 1,230 carts, 2,400 cattle and horses, and were assessed seven times, totaling over 122,500 yuan in silver. The cost of wheat was over 82,700 yuan in silver, and the combined cost of firewood and fodder was over 120,700 yuan in silver. The loss from unofficial requisitions is estimated to be over 80,000 yuan, with over 2,000 people fleeing and 3,102 laborers conscripted. This year's wheat harvest averaged less than 30%, all of which was used for supplies. With prolonged drought and no hope for the autumn harvest, the survivors of the calamity are crying out in anguish. Furthermore, Tongxu County, bordering the front line, although not a formal war zone, has suffered enormous losses from the continuous passage of large armies over the past few months. According to the people of the county, they were required to supply 1,955 carts, 8,101 cattle and horses, with property losses amounting to 520,430 yuan. There were five assessments totaling over 57,824 yuan in silver. Grain and food cost over 126,902 yuan in silver, and firewood cost over 31,330 yuan in silver. There were 3,597 laborers conscripted. This year's wheat harvest averaged about 30%, but the supply losses were so immense. With drought followed by floods, there is little hope for the autumn harvest. The means of survival are exhausted, and cries for help are endless. The Henan Relief Committee has telegraphed the military authorities and various benevolent organizations in the north and south about the disaster situation in Chenliu and Tongxu, requesting assistance and relief.

Guangzhou Tobacco Guild Requests Amendment to Sino-Egyptian Treaty

Special Clause Affects Exports of Domestic Goods Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangdong Tobacco Guild states that the Sino-Egyptian Treaty was originally intended to be based on the principle of mutual benefit. However, a special clause added to the treaty hinders the export of Guangdong tobacco to Egypt, causing losses to agriculture, industry, and commerce. They have petitioned the Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce to forward their request to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government for a prompt amendment or extension of the implementation period of the special clause to protect national rights. The original text states, "The Egyptian government has signed treaties with China, Denmark, Switzerland, Belgium, and other countries, all based on the principle of mutual benefit, and promulgated the provisions. However, for China, the provisions state that 'If either party wishes to cancel this temporary agreement during its term, it must notify the other party three months in advance.' Underneath this, it adds the clause: 'However, on February 16, 1931, this agreement must be rendered invalid according to the Egyptian Customs Law No. 2 promulgated in 1930.' Reading this translation is deeply shocking. The main Chinese goods exported to Egypt are natural products, such as tobacco produced in Guangdong Province, with very large sales volumes. However, the process from planting tobacco to shipping it takes six to seven months to complete. If the term of the current treaty is limited, the tobacco prepared for export to Egypt will inevitably not be shipped in time. This would cause enormous losses to agriculture, industry, and commerce. If the deadline is exceeded, the customs law will treat it as if it were from a non-treaty country, and taxes will be doubled. In the future, the export of domestic goods will be severely affected. Moreover, countries such as the United States, Switzerland, Denmark, and Belgium do not have this clause, and it is specifically applied to China. This makes the treaty equivalent to no treaty, which is particularly embarrassing in terms of national dignity. Therefore, we jointly submit this petition to your chamber, respectfully requesting that you consider it, forward it to the Construction Department and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government, and urge them to amend the special clause added to the Sino-Egyptian Treaty or extend the implementation period in advance to protect commerce and national integrity." The General Chamber of Commerce, upon learning of the situation, deemed it related to foreign treaties and has forwarded the case to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review and handling.

Guangdong Province Cleans Up the Guangzhou Branch of the Industrial and Commercial Bank

The Court Organizes a Liquidation Committee

Guangzhou dispatch: After the provincial government decided to allocate the Guangzhou branch of the Industrial and Commercial Bank to the High Court to organize a liquidation committee, the High Court immediately dispatched a chief clerk of the court, together with the president of the District Court, a chief prosecutor of the District Court, two prosecutors, a chief clerk, and two presiding judges. It also appointed the dean of the Faculty of Law of Zhongshan University and the director of the Central Bank, totaling ten people, to establish a committee to liquidate the Guangzhou branch of the Industrial and Commercial Bank on the 25th. Yao Lixiu, the dean of the Faculty of Law of Zhongshan University, was publicly elected as the chairman of the committee. They have already started to work and have sent letters to the General Chamber of Commerce and creditors to each send a representative to attend the meetings. Yesterday, they, together with the representative of the Public Security Bureau, Mr. Ling, and Mr. Liang of the Taiping Police Sub-station, went to the bank to receive all documents and books. The representative of the Public Security Bureau handed over one bundle of documents and sixteen keys that he had been holding. The general manager of the bank, Chen Guoxuan, and the deputy general manager, Ouyang Qi, handed over the bank's cash, books, furniture, and other items, which were all received one by one. The committee has reported the inventory to the provincial government for review. It is reported that the committee is conducting various matters separately and has announced that the period from September 1st to 30th is the deadline for reporting claims, requiring all creditors to report their names and the amount of debt within the prescribed period. According to the committee's recent investigation, the Guangzhou branch of the Industrial and Commercial Bank owes approximately 500,000 yuan, and the amount of loans issued is approximately 170,000 yuan. Over 50,000 yuan of loans have been recovered in recent days and temporarily stored in the Central Bank for distribution after the liquidation is completed. According to the committee, the liquidation will take at least two months because it will take time to recover loans and auction off assets. As for the amount to be repaid to creditors, the estimated amount is at least 30%. (August 30th)

Zhejiang Province Rectifies Long-Standing Abuses in Taxation

The Zhejiang Provincial Government considers that the province's military and administrative expenses are vast, but the collection of regular and miscellaneous taxes by various counties is often ineffective, with delayed remittances and unauthorized misappropriation of tax funds, resulting in unclear accounts. These various long-standing abuses affect revenue and cause the provincial treasury to be frequently depleted. In order to rectify this situation, in addition to dispatching eight people from the Finance Department, including Wang Xianjie, Zhou Xinyuan, Yao Chongjiang, Yi Yang, Xiu Yanyan, Deng Shiqiao, Qiu Zhenglun, and Chen Mianyun, to various counties to investigate and supervise collection, it has also formulated measures to rectify the collection and remittance of taxes by various counties, ordering all county governments and finance bureaus to strictly comply. The measures are as follows: (1) Special regulations are established for the collection of land tax, deed tax, tooth tax, pawnbroker tax, and slaughter tax in each county. It is essential to collect the full amount within the prescribed time limit. If there is a shortfall due to delays, the Finance Department will assess and list the responsible officials for severe punishment according to regulations. (2) Tax revenues should be remitted promptly, and it is forbidden to withhold or deposit them. The amount of taxes collected in the first month should be remitted immediately once a certain amount is accumulated. The remaining amount should be remitted to the treasury before the 5th of the second month. Any delays will be dealt with severely by the Finance Department according to the regulations on delayed remittance of land tax by counties. (3) Counties often misappropriate funds earmarked for the province without approval, and then use other uses as excuses after being urged, hindering provincial revenue. This is unacceptable. In the future, the provincial funds should not be misappropriated without prior approval. Violations will be treated as embezzlement of public funds, and the perpetrators will be held responsible for compensation. For funds that have already been misappropriated, they must be repaid in full within one month. Any delays will be investigated by the Finance Department and reported for punishment. (4) Counties should pay the allocated funds upon receiving notification and immediately submit a general receipt to the treasury. Delays are not allowed. Violations will be investigated and punished by the Finance Department. (5) Whenever a collecting official in a county is replaced, the collected funds should be cleared on the date of handover, and all funds due to the province should be fully remitted. If, at the time of accounting, it is found that 1,000 yuan or more of the funds to be remitted has been withheld, the Finance Department will investigate and report for severe punishment. If they are transferred to another county, they must not go to the assigned post before remitting the funds due to the province in full. The Finance Department should investigate and report such cases to the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs for immediate detention. (6) Counties should submit the land tax monthly report and various monthly report forms before the 5th of the following month. However, counties often delay and hold them back for months, which is a violation. In the future, the regulations must be strictly followed, and the reports must be submitted on time for assessment. Failure to submit them for a long time will be investigated by the Finance Department and reported for punishment.

Local Communications Songjiang

Hu's Murder of Wife Case Exposed Hu Yinglong, from Taiwu Bridge, is thirty years old and has inherited three households. He married Zhang from the city three years ago. There was no affection between them, and they had no children. Hu's widowed aunt, Nie, always favored Hu Yinglong and treated the daughter-in-law coldly. It is easy to imagine the family's situation. However, on the evening of the 30th of last month, Zhang suddenly died violently. On the morning of the 31st, her maternal family arrived and heard rumors from neighbors. They became suspicious of the death, leading to a suspicious case. Yesterday, Zhang Zeshen and Zhang Zeyu, the younger brothers of the deceased, hired lawyer Wang Tinggan to write a petition asking the prosecutor's office to investigate thoroughly. The gist of the petition was that the deceased was envied by her mother-in-law, Nie, from the night of her wedding to Hu Yinglong, and the couple and the mother-in-law were constantly at odds. There were deep rope marks on the deceased's neck, which were now blue-purple, and knife wounds. Her limbs were bent, and both wrists were blue-purple and swollen, indicating that they were forcibly held by an accomplice. It was obviously a murder. At the time of the interaction, the Hu family separated my mother and us and persuaded us to stop, so we could not discuss the matter and report it, and the coffin was hastily prepared. When the coffin was carried out, the neighbors protested loudly, intending to redress the grievance of the deceased. When we returned to hold a family meeting, everyone said that since there were obvious injuries, we should seek justice. Therefore, we asked lawyer Wang to file a complaint. Yesterday (the 3rd) afternoon, after receiving the petition, the prosecutor's office immediately arrested the defendant and conducted a preliminary hearing. Hu Yinglong's testimony was reportedly evasive. Then, the plaintiff was questioned as to why he did not report it before the encoffining. According to the testimony, when we heard the news and went to see, we felt suspicious, but we were persuaded by the Hu family clan leader Runzhang and his brothers, and other female Hu relatives, to stop my mother, so we could not meet and discuss the report. It was ordered that the coffin be opened for examination today. The burial site is at the Data Bang in Shishi Yitu outside the North Gate. The prosecutor, accompanied by the clerk, examiners, and doctors Ke Haiqiong and Zhang Shaoxiu, went to examine the body. Hu Yinglong was also taken by the police. At the time of this reporter's writing, the examination had just been completed and returned to the court. For a while, the onlookers were blocked, inquiring about the examination results. Although no official announcement has been made, it is reported that there were three fingerprints on the neck. Hu Yinglong initially denied it, but when his fingers matched, he admitted that he was temporarily confused.

Wuxi

Robbery of Commercial Ship, Five Robbers Arrested The Xicheng line of Licheng Shipping Company's Wuxi-Cheng boat, under the Gongyun Bridge in Xiyi, departed from Cheng at around 10 o'clock the night before last. When it arrived under the railway bridge near Gaoqiao, seven or eight robbers with guns shouted to stop the ship and fired warning shots. The driver, seeing this, stopped and docked the ship. Just as the robbers were about to board the ship to rob it, more than ten armed soldiers suddenly rushed over. It turned out that a squad of military police was stationed under the Gaoqiao Bridge and came after hearing the gunshots. The soldiers rushed to the railway bridge and saw that it was a robbery of a ship. They immediately went forward to arrest them and caught five robbers on the spot: Shi Jincai, Yang Shouchong, Xia Peifu, Chen Er, and Zhang Yaer. Five fake pistols and a string of small firecrackers were found on their bodies. They were immediately presented to the regiment headquarters for interrogation. The robbers' statements were cunning, and they all denied the robbery. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be temporarily detained pending further investigation.

Transfer Clerk Absconds with Funds Tang Junyuan, alias A Gou, 21 years old, a transfer clerk at the Gongyun Bridge Public Welfare Transfer Company outside the Guangfu Gate in this city, recently became involved with Sanbao, a female worker at a silk factory, and became very particular about clothing, food, housing, and transportation, which led to increased expenses and financial difficulties. At the end of last month, he secretly took the bankbook and withdrew a large sum of money from various banks, totaling 700 silver yuan from Yuanchang, 300 silver yuan from Baokangrun, and 500 silver yuan from Fuyuan, for a total of 1,500 silver yuan. After Tang withdrew the money, he went to the company to pack his clothes and falsely claimed to Chen Zikun, the manager, that he needed three days of leave. He then absconded with Sanbao. Chen Zikun learned of this yesterday and immediately sent an express letter to Junyuan's father in Hankou and sent people to Suzhou, Shanghai, and other places to search for him.

Robbery Victim Shoots and Kills Bandit Leader In Yanjia Dang, District 16 (Wan'an City), of this county, there are more than 30 households. Yan Liqing is the deputy township head and comes from a wealthy family. At about 2:00 a.m. the night before last, three or four boats suddenly arrived in the village, carrying more than 20 bandits with seven or eight guns. They rushed ashore and first went to the home of Yan Asheng. They tied up Yan's hands and asked where Yan Liqing's house was. Yan Asheng replied that it was over a few houses. The bandits left him and rushed to Yan Liqing's house. When they found the door closed, they had difficulty breaking it down. A bandit leader climbed over the wall and onto the roof, intending to open the door from inside. At this time, Yan Wenyuan, the son of Liqing, was awakened from the wheat and immediately took his self-defense rifle and went out. He saw a bandit on the roof and immediately fired, hitting the bandit in the head. The bandit immediately fell to the roof and died. The other bandits were terrified when they heard the gunshot from the victim's family and left in a hurry. Yesterday, the county government sent an investigator to the village to investigate.

Zhenjiang

The Finance Department has set a deadline for various counties to complete outstanding handover procedures. In Jiangsu Province, there are a total of 58 counties and over 300 former magistrates, county heads, or heads of finance bureaus who have not completed their handover procedures. Previously, the provincial government decided to strictly pursue these matters and instructed the Finance Department to handle them. Now, Director Chen of the Finance Department has copied the names of officials from various counties who have outstanding handover procedures or unpaid debts and issued a public notice, ordering them to promptly proceed to their respective counties to jointly calculate and settle accounts with the current county head or head of the finance bureau in accordance with regulations. From the date of this announcement, they have one month to calculate and report the settlement. Those who have already jointly calculated but have not paid their debts must also pay the full amount within one month.

The Provincial Reorganization Committee Reduces the Number of Routine Meetings. The Jiangsu Provincial Party Reorganization Committee's meeting dates were previously Wednesdays and Saturdays. Now, due to the need for lengthy and careful consideration in designating executive and supervisory committee members for various counties, as well as supplementing personnel for the Party Reorganization Committee in various counties and reviewing other important cases, it is heard that for the sake of facilitating work, the Saturday meeting has been changed to a discussion meeting, allowing for a more relaxed discussion of important cases. It is also heard that this reform will be implemented starting this week.

Rickshaw Pullers Petition for Price Reduction. Representatives of Zhenjiang rickshaw pullers, including Sun Bingquan, have, with the intention of relieving the suffering of rickshaw pullers, instructed rickshaw companies to reduce fares, effective August 1st. However, the rickshaw companies petitioned the authorities to withdraw the price reduction order and have also placed numerous obstacles in the way of rickshaw pullers owning their own vehicles. They have jointly submitted a petition to the Provincial Public Security Bureau yesterday, with the following five objectives: (1) Immediately implement the price reduction ordered by the Construction Department; (2) Rickshaw companies must refund all overcharges collected after August 1st; (3) The quota for rickshaws in the provincial capital is 1,000 vehicles, and there are currently 678 vehicles. The remaining 322 vehicles should all be allowed to be owned by rickshaw pullers, eliminating exploitation; otherwise, please allow the 100 rickshaws already owned by rickshaw pullers to operate earlier; (4) Licenses for rickshaws owned by rickshaw pullers should be granted upon application; (5) Allow the organization of an association to prevent the infiltration and incitement of reactionary elements.

Liu Hai Sha Captures Bandits and Sends Them to the Province. The Public Security Bureau of the Liu Hai Sha District Office has sent the four captured bandits, Huang Kui, Zhou Zhao, Chen Zirong, and Guo Shaoshan, to the county government and then to the Provincial Bandit Suppression Headquarters for interrogation.

The Case of the Car Company Owner's Tragic Death is Adjudicated. Jiang Chuntang, the owner of the Lu Gu Car Company in the New Market in Chengnan, was tragically beaten to death because the county police team sealed off hired cars. The county court has concluded the trial of the criminals in this case and sentenced Wang Hongchen to three years and six months of imprisonment for the crime of joint injury causing death, and Zhao Changyi to one year and nine months of imprisonment for the crime of assisting in injury causing death, with a three-year suspended sentence.

Jiangyin

Execution of Accomplices Chen Wei Wu and Yu Bing Qing. Farmers from Qiaoqi Rizhao Township captured the communist leader Chen Wei Wu at the Zhulin Nunnery. After repeated interrogations by the county government and accusations by the Party, it was found that reactionary elements were rampant in the urban area. A search of six schools outside the city resulted in the arrest of Xu Yan Ji and Hua, who had all held important positions in government agencies. Both had served as directors of the Municipal Administration Bureau and were currently members of the Chamber of Commerce and assistants in a district office. The Provincial Government and the Provincial Party Department were furious at the rampant reactionary forces in Jiangyin and immediately sent a committee to conduct an interrogation. They returned to the province the day before yesterday (the 3rd) to report. Yesterday, County Magistrate Li received telegrams from both the Provincial Government and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stating that the communist Chen Wei Wu had repeatedly participated in riots and that his confession was confirmed. He should be sentenced to death. The bandit Yu Bing Qing, nicknamed Big Head Ah Bing, had repeatedly committed arson and murder, confessed without denial, and should also be sentenced to death. After receiving the telegrams, County Magistrate Li ordered the police team to bring Chen and Yu to the barren land behind Zhongshan Park at Jin Gang Tui around 3 PM and execute them by firing squad. It was raining heavily at the time, and the onlookers were as numerous as a wall. Chen's body was collected by his mother, Chen Ji Shi. Chen had been working in the education sector for many years and lived in the Qianjie neighborhood of the county, and was 27 years old.

Ningbo

The Yin Feng Road Xikou Section Is Operating Normally. The section of the Yin Feng Road from Xikou to Dabu Tou was washed away by floods in July, causing it to be impassable. It is now heard that the road surface has been repaired and has been operating normally since the 31st of last month.

Smugglers Attack Smuggling Suppression Team. The Taojia Peng area of Dinghai County has been stationed by the fourth team of the Smuggling Suppression Team. Unexpectedly, at around 1 PM on the afternoon of last month (July) 30th, over thirty smugglers rushed into the team's office, intending to seize weapons. Fortunately, the team leader, Zhao Cheng, had taken precautions and immediately dispersed the smugglers. However, the smugglers were unwilling to submit and gathered fifty to sixty people to fight again an hour later. Both sides opened fire. The officers and soldiers were outnumbered and were killed Huang Dafu, one soldier, and over ten were seriously injured. Afterwards, Team Leader Zhao led his troops to bravely resist and finally repelled the smugglers, capturing four ringleaders: Zhang Pingnan, Wang Qiaoxian, Ni Ajin, and Liu Sifu. Due to the seriousness of the case, the captured criminals were sent to the provincial capital for interrogation.

Hangzhou

The Bandit Suppression Headquarters Expands. The Bandit Suppression Headquarters of Ning Shao Wen Tai in Zhejiang Province has been designated as the second district by the provincial government. Commander Gan still governs Ning Shao Wen Tai. Now, with the frequent banditry in eastern Zhejiang, a plan is being devised to thoroughly eradicate it. The Bandit Suppression Headquarters should be expanded. In addition to Wang Wenhan continuing to serve as the commanding officer, Gan Qingchi, the commander of the 4th Security Regiment, and Liu Xiwun, the commander of the 1st Regiment, were appointed as deputy commanders yesterday, so that command can be implemented thoroughly and support can be provided to each other.

Eradicating Bandits and Communists in Wenzhou and Chu. The Zhejiang Provincial Government, in order to thoroughly eradicate banditry, yesterday specifically ordered Wang Wenhan, the bandit suppression commander of the four prefectures, to quickly lead the protection team from the Zhenhai Fortress Command, one battalion from the 6th Security Regiment, two companies from the 5th Regiment, and a mortar company to join forces with the offshore water police to work hard to suppress the bandits, and must completely eradicate them in the shortest possible time in order to quell banditry and quiet the local area.

Zhu Jia Hua Will Go to Guangdong Soon. Zhu Jia Hua, the Director of Civil Affairs of Zhejiang Province, has repeatedly received telegrams from Zhongshan University in Guangdong urging him to go to Guangdong quickly to deal with everything related to the school's affairs. After receiving the telegrams, Zhu decided to take a boat to Guangdong from Shanghai within a few days, and will return to Zhejiang in about half a month.

Hefei

Bandits and Communists Rampant in Shou and Lu Counties. A large gang of bandits is entrenched in the Shuangmiao Ji area in the southern countryside of Shou County, robbing and kidnapping people. The 5th District Bandit Suppression Commander, Song Shike, has sent a large force from Shou County to suppress them. On the 30th, he also telegraphed Cheng Yi, the commander of the 1st Regiment stationed in Feicheng, to lead his troops to intercept them from Feicheng. Commander Cheng is currently leading Wang Zhenwu's battalion to attack from Xia Tang Ji. In addition, bandits and communists are rampant in the Ke Jia Tan and Ma Cao Shan areas in the western countryside of Lujiang County. Repeated telegrams have been sent to Commander Song Shike, requesting that troops be sent to suppress them. It is heard that it has been decided to send a battalion within a few days, taking the route through Sanhe.

Gui and Shen were detained entirely due to the Yangguang Society case and have no connection to the Da Bao. He has entrusted me to send a letter of correction. I hope you will publish it as a favor. Lawyer Wang Youlin, September 4th.

Special Item

Report on the Participation of the National Private Electric Power Association in the World Power Conference, by Li Yanshi and Shen Sifang

Yanshi, Sifang, and others, as representatives of this association, attended the Second World Power Conference in Berlin, Germany. We departed at the end of April and passed through Little Luzon and Singapore, where we received warm hospitality from Consuls Li and Tang. We took the opportunity to investigate the state of the electric power industry in both locations. On the ship, we also met with Consul Shen of Medan, who agreed to investigate the electric power situation in the Dutch East Indies archipelago on our behalf. We arrived in Genoa, Italy in early June. We stayed there for a day and, with the introduction of our acting consul, visited an electric factory. Then we went to Switzerland to meet Fei Fushou, an engineer from the Suzhou Electric Factory. Mr. Fei was one of the representatives sent by this association to attend the Power Conference in Berlin. We stayed in Switzerland for a day and then went to the Berlin Power Conference office. They had been informed of our arrival in Germany in advance and sent a special staff to greet us at the station. Newspaper reporters came to inquire about the news. We were determined to conduct on-the-spot investigations and did not want to overdo the publicity, so we dealt with them briefly. Government representatives Huang Boqiao and Wang Shengsan had arrived in Germany in advance, and Zhu Maocheng and Wu Keyu also arrived successively. Representatives of our association, Yao Kewen from the Jiujiang Electric Company and Zhou Maobai from the Hanyang Electric Company, also came to the meeting. Ambassador Jiang to Germany gave a special welcome banquet. At the same time, the German Eastern Association, various industrial groups, and various companies that had dealings with our country in the past competed to host banquets. It was difficult to attend so many events. At the same time, Ambassador Jiang, in view of the small number of representatives from our country, appointed more than ten students studying abroad to assist in everything and to attend the conference as observers in order to enhance our prestige. Thus, a delegation was formed and a communications office was established. Before the opening of the conference, the delegation held a meeting to exchange views. We were fortunate that the sentiments and views of the representatives were harmonious and consistent with the goals of our association. The Power Conference was initiated by the Englishman Dunlop. Its purpose was to create an international organization to discuss and study various important issues of power economics. In 1924, the founding conference was held in England. Representatives of electric factories from various countries, as well as scientists, technicians, and economists, all attended the meeting. They conducted a general study of the sources of power and its development in industry, transportation, and economy. Afterwards, a partial meeting was held once a year to discuss matters such as hydropower generation, the regulation of electricity, and fuel issues, rotating in various countries. Last year, a partial meeting of the Power Conference was held at the same time as the Japan International Industrial Conference. This conference, in addition to concluding the affairs of previous partial meetings, further explored the entire power issue, paying particular attention to the distribution of power and the economic issues of using power. Therefore, economic principles were the major premise of this meeting. We, having understood the purpose of the Power Conference, attended the group meetings after the opening. From June 16th to 26th, the discussions were divided into 18 categories: (1) The use of electricity, (2) The manufacture and application of gas, (3) The use and transmission of power, (4) Thermal power plants, (5) Prime movers, (6) The economics of solid fuels, (7) Boilers, (8) Internal combustion engines, (9) Hydropower plants and their economic equipment, (10) The development and regulation of incoming power, (11) Storage and regulation of electricity, (12) Generators, (13) Distribution equipment, (14) The transmission of electricity, (15) Economic load ratio and electricity prices of power plants, (16) The supply and regulation of power, (17) Power in transportation, (18) Research on standard statistics education. There were 3,900 representatives from 34 countries, which was a grand event of the time. A total of 392 papers were presented, and the essence was extracted to form 34 general reports, which were presented, read, and discussed one by one. This kind of report, regarding the recent state of various aspects of world power issues, gave us a deep understanding, which was indeed rare. Especially in our country, where agriculture is declining and industry is nascent, national power, animal power, and human power account for a large part. How should we use natural resources, coal, oil, and hydropower, to generate power to meet all needs? Which should come first, which should come later, which is economical and effective, which is futile and ineffective, which should be promoted by the state, and which should be operated by the people? Furthermore, in view of the fact that electricity is the most economical and convenient power source, and that electricity accounts for a large part of the statistics of the world's power development, if we want to develop our country's agriculture and industry, if we want to build China, in other words, if we want to save China, it will not be possible without developing the electrical industry. This association is the only major gathering of the national electrical industry. Its future work is complex and extensive. The mission it shoulders is heavy and significant. Its relationship with the Power Conference is deep and significant. We are talented but inexperienced. We have accepted the responsibility of being representatives. We only have to humbly lower our hearts, not hold preconceived notions, and discuss with representatives from advanced countries. We will collect works. It is a very long story, and we will wait until another day to write a special book for the reference of colleagues across the country. Now we would like to report the general results of the Second Power Conference as follows: (1) There were more than 3,000 experts attending the conference. Because of the cutting, grinding, and viewing, emotions were generated, and international goodwill was also improved. (2) Use technical methods to reduce the cost of electricity, improve the load situation, and promote the cooperation of the electric power industry. As a result, the people can enjoy the benefits of cheap electricity. (3) The supply of power is more complete, and the methods of making goods from raw materials are also increasing. Each new method requires the employment of a new job. The increase in these new jobs can offset the number of people reduced by machines and more. Therefore, the more natural power is used, the fewer unemployed workers there will be. (4) After the European War, due to changes in technical and economic conditions, the issue of whether the electrical industry should be run commercially or officially also arose. Politicians have recognized that the electrical industry must be managed by the government. Economists mostly hold the opposite view and advocate commercial operation. This conference also discussed this issue in depth. As a result, the majority still supports commercial operation. At a minimum, only a small number of joint ventures between the government and businesses are considered feasible. After the Power Conference closed, the Rhine River Group visited major German industries, such as brown coal mines, steel mills, paint factories, and motor manufacturing factories. After a period of more than a month, we can report the following: (To be continued)

Educational News Highlights

The National Government's Resolution on the National Education and Culture Budget

The Ministry of Education previously submitted a report to the Executive Yuan, stating that the national education and culture budget for the 19th year that should be compiled by the ministry has been compiled in accordance with regulations and sent to the Ministry of Finance for review on May 31st. The budget for the 19th year of national universities, national specialized schools, and the National Beiyang Institute of Technology has been changed compared with the approved budget for the 18th year due to factual necessity. The 19th year has already begun, and the schools are proceeding separately according to the planned construction plan, including adding classes and supplementing equipment, and have started preparations according to the 19th year budget standard. However, because the budget has not been approved, the school administration is extremely difficult. We have repeatedly requested that the budget be approved in advance. It is appropriate to request that your court review and approve and forward the budget for the 19th year of each school to the Central Political Conference in advance. It is heard that the government and court will handle the expenses of each school as before until the new budget is officially announced, and regarding the cultural budget, the National Government ordered the Executive Yuan to write a letter saying that the Central Political Conference had approved the letter from the Ministry of Finance approving the Ministry of Education's transmission of the budget for national education and culture for the 19th year and requested that it be reviewed and forwarded. The total expenditures listed in the second-level expenditure budget for education and culture for the 19th year compiled by the Ministry of Education, in addition to the Central Education Museum as a new business, and the year before last as a regular expense, a total of 13,712,055 yuan has been reviewed and approved by the Finance Committee one after another. The total expenditure for the current year is 17,140,645 yuan, an increase of 3,428,590 yuan compared with the approved total for the previous year. The recurring expenses of the Ministry of Education have also increased by 108,000 yuan. At a time when finances are difficult and national treasury expenditures are huge, it seems inappropriate to expand the budget for military and political expenses in the 19th year. Should this education and culture budget be appropriately reduced so that the financial education business of the country can be planned and taken care of? We will send the original budget for your review and so on. The case was handed over to the Finance Group for review, and the reply stated that the implementation details of the 19th year budget relief measures have been reviewed and deemed feasible. Please follow the procedure in the case of the national education and culture budget so as to be unified. Is it appropriate? Please make a public decision, etc. The conference decided to handle it according to the review opinions. The implementation details of the 19th year budget relief measures have been communicated in another document. It is appropriate to record the case and send the original printed letter from the Ministry of Finance for your reference and instruct the Ministry of Finance to comply with it, etc. Attached is a copy of the original letter.

The Ministry of Education Distributes the Primer-Marked Version of Sun Yat-sen's Testament

The Ministry of Education has distributed a primer-marked version of Sun Yat-sen's testament to promote it widely, sending letters to all agencies inside and outside Beijing (inside Beijing refers to the central party and government agencies, and outside Beijing refers to the provincial and municipal governments). The letter stated that Sun Yat-sen's testament should be popularized as soon as possible, so that every household in the country knows about it. Now is the time to promote the primer-mark system, and we should use this system to help popularize the testament. We have now annotated the text of Sun Yat-sen's testament with primer-marks, character by character, to facilitate the learning and recitation of the general public and the promotion of various agencies. The printing has now been completed, and we are sending several copies. Please check and paste them in your agency and forward them to your subordinates for posting. If there are not enough, please imitate and print them to promote them widely. In addition, the four tones marked by this foreign sound are annotated according to the standard sounds set by the National Language Unification Preparation Committee of the Ministry of Education. If the four tones are not marked in local letters, please check it out.

The Zhejiang Department of Education Issues Standards for Administrative Implementation

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, in order to have a basis for the implementation of education in various counties and cities, has specifically formulated standards for the implementation of educational administration and sent them to various counties and cities for compliance. The original text is as follows: (1) Each county and city department should establish an obligatory education committee and a popular education committee, (2) The supervisors and instructors of each county and city should, in accordance with the resolutions of the provincial local education guidance conference, formulate a supervision plan based on local conditions, (3) The experimental schools, central schools, and popular schools in each county and city should discuss experimental matters and guidance steps, (4) Each county and city should organize and establish a primary school education research association. Those who have organized and established one should determine the research center and make further explorations, (5) Each county should formulate measures to reward and ban private primary schools, (6) Each county and city should formulate measures to improve private schools, (7) Each county and city education bureau or education department should organize a Party theory research association and a reading club.

### The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Request for a Mandatory Education Law

Instruction from the Ministry of Education: Postponed for Further Discussion

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to forward to the central government a proposal to quickly enact a mandatory education law. The Ministry of Education has now instructed the bureau, stating: "We have received your submission. It goes without saying that mandatory education is urgently needed. However, considering the current economic situation in various parts of our country, it is difficult to universally enforce compulsory school attendance at this time. Your request to have the Ministry forward a proposal to the central government to quickly enact a mandatory education law with clear penalties should be postponed for further discussion. As for piloting mandatory education in certain areas, it is feasible to first establish compulsory measures within a possible scope, considering local conditions. The bureau may draft specific regulations for the pilot implementation of mandatory education in the Lu Xing District and submit them for approval." This order is issued.

He did not meet with the Director but will visit again in the coming days to seek a satisfactory outcome.

News from Yesterday's Literacy Campaign in the Counties

The literacy campaign was held in the Shanghai counties in separate districts yesterday and the day before. The following is a brief record of the second and third districts: Second District: The meeting place was originally scheduled for the Public Sports Field. The speaker's platform and all arrangements had been completed. However, a heavy rain suddenly fell at the time (afternoon of the 2nd), so the meeting was temporarily moved to the Public Tea Garden. About 200 people, including residents and students from various schools, attended the meeting. Lin Qing, representing the Education Bureau, presided over the meeting and delivered the opening remarks. Representatives from the County Reorganization Committee (Chen), the District Chief (Peng Zhao-tang), various organizations, and schools then gave speeches. The speeches were lengthy and are not recorded here. District Chief Peng's speech was particularly good because his language was colloquial and he cited many examples of successful adult learners who were familiar to the audience, which was very effective. The meeting adjourned at around 5 p.m. Third District: The meeting was held at the Central Tea Garden in Beiqiao Town at 2 p.m. on the afternoon of the 3rd. Despite the heavy rain, attendance still reached over 100 people due to sufficient prior publicity and entertainment. District Chief Yang Fu-lin presided over the meeting and gave a report. Representatives from the County Government, the County Reorganization Committee, the Public Security Bureau (Fu Dian-ying, Chen Jia-pu), and various organizations and schools then gave speeches. Finally, the Jin brothers from the Agricultural Education Center performed a two-person comic dialogue that used allegories about the pain of illiteracy to add to the amusement. The meeting adjourned at around 4 p.m.

Shanghai County Public Night School Scheduled to Open

Preparations for the public night school affiliated with the Shanghai County Government and its subordinate bureaus have been underway for a long time. It is now understood that all matters have been completed, and the school is scheduled to open at 7 p.m. on the 15th of this month. The school's regulations are recorded below: (1) To provide employees of various agencies with the opportunity to receive education outside of work hours. (2) The subjects are Party Principles, Mandarin Chinese, Arithmetic, and General Knowledge. (3) All employees of various agencies, regardless of whether they are literate or not, can enroll. (4) Tuition is free, and school supplies are provided by the school. (5) The duration of study is four months. A graduation certificate is issued upon passing the examination at the end of the study period. (6) Classes are held every evening from 7 p.m. to 9 p.m. (7) The school is located at the Shanghai County Government.

Meeting Minutes for the Commemoration of Yuan Guanlan

Organizing Compulsory Education Zones

Preparing a Memorial Service

Full Meeting on the 7th of this Month

The China Vocational Education Society held a meeting yesterday (3rd) at 3 p.m. at the Vocational Education Society to commemorate Mr. Yuan Guanlan. Attendees included Qian Xin-zhi, Zhou Jing-han, Jia Ji-ying, Ruan Jie-fan, Zhang Gong-quan, Jiang Wen-yu, Huang Ren-zhi, Yang Wei-yu, Zhao Shi-fu, Shen Yi-zhen, Wang Dian-cun, Wang Feng-gu, Wang Zhi-xin, Shen Xin-qing, Wang Yong-ren, Jiang Zhu-zhuang, Yuan Zhong-lian, Yuan Shu-yu, Pan Yang-yao, and Lu Gui-liang. Shen Xin-qing was elected as chairman, and the ceremony was conducted according to protocol. The chairman declared the purpose of commemorating Mr. Yuan. Then, attendees expressed their opinions. Finally, it was resolved to establish a Mr. Yuan Guanlan Memorial Committee, with Shen Xin-qing as chairman, Jiang Wen-yu as treasurer, and Yang Wei-yu as secretary. Jiang Dian-cun, Huang Ren-zhi, and Jiang Zhu-zhuang will organize compulsory education zones. Wang Yong-ren, Wang Feng-gu, Qing Jie-ying, Zhu Jing-nong, Gu Yin-ting, Zhang Gong-quan, Jiang Wen-yu, Huang Ren-zhi, Lu Gui-liang, Gu Shu-zhi, Qin Feng-xiang, and Yang Wei-yu were appointed as members to prepare for the memorial service. Wang Feng-gu, Ruan Jie-fan, Shen Yi-zhen, Pu Jie-ying, Zhao Shi-fu, Jia Ji-ying, Chen Ji-cheng, Cheng Shi-sheng, Huang Ren-zhi, Yang Wei-yu, and Yan Du-he were appointed as preparatory members. Zhang Gong-quan will be in charge of preparing commemorative objects in the Baoshan area. Jiang Wen-yu will contact the principal of Shanghai High School in the Longmen area. Jia Ji-ying, Chen Ji-cheng, Cheng Shi-sheng, Wang Feng-gu, and Yao Hui-quan will be in charge of the preparations. Wang Dian-cun will be in charge of collecting posthumous works, relics, and anecdotes. It was also decided that the second full committee meeting would be held at the Vocational Education Society at 3 p.m. on the 7th of this month. In addition to those who have already been invited and those who attended today, it was resolved to add Cai Zi-min, Mu Chu, Yao Zi-rang, Ye Li-wen, Zou Bing-wen, Shi Liang-cai, Qing Jie-ying, Gu Zhen-yi, Wu Shi-qiao, Tao Hui-min, Yin Xiang-sun, Jin Ju-shan, Shan Zhan-yun, Pan Zhong-ang, Zhu Bu-lan, Jin Jing-yang, Xia Lang-yun, Pan Xu-lun, and Shi Yang-yong as members of the committee.

Anti-Drug Association Promotes Anti-Drug Education

In order to promote student participation in the anti-drug movement and implement anti-drug education policies, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association will publish a monthly anti-drug magazine and various series of novels. The association will actively promote these publications to schools across the country to achieve widespread reach. In addition, the association will hold essay competitions and an anti-drug speech contest in Shanghai. The contest has already been held three times. Local branches also hold contests annually in their respective areas. The Anti-Drug Association has begun preparations for this year's speech contest and is inviting prominent figures from the national government and enthusiastic individuals from home and abroad to donate prizes to encourage participation. It is expected that schools will soon be invited to join. Provincial and municipal branches have been notified by the association to follow suit. Furthermore, the association has repeatedly promoted the inclusion of anti-drug materials in textbooks. The association drafted a proposal that was discussed and approved for implementation at the First National Anti-Smoking Conference. However, many newly published textbooks do not include these materials. To promote the implementation of this plan, the association's education department has been tasked with collecting all historical information about the anti-drug movement and other drug-related events that can serve as teaching materials for textbooks. The association will compile this information and submit it separately to various publishing houses for inclusion in reprints or new compilations. It is reported that the association has also requested that government authorities include the date of the annual anti-drug week on calendars to indicate its permanence. The Ministry of Education has forwarded this request to the Astronomical Institute of the Academia Sinica for processing. The Shanghai branch has also requested that the Social Bureau include the date in the new calendars it prints, and this has been approved. It is reported that the association also plans to promote the realization of this plan soon.

Development of Huiling Middle School

Since its establishment, the New Longhua Huiling Middle School has been actively undergoing reorganization and has been praised by local residents. Principal Qian is paying attention to school hygiene and student convenience. He is raising significant funds to build water and electricity infrastructure. Water wells have been dug and completed, and electric lights have been installed. The school is currently in contact with the China General Edison Company to connect the power lines and provide electricity in the near future. Several renowned teachers have also been newly hired to improve the quality of teaching. As a result, enrollment for the current semester is very enthusiastic. It is reported that school will begin on the 10th, registration will be on the 11th, and classes will start on the 12th.

Appointments of Faculty and Staff at Jiangnan College

Since the establishment of Jiangnan College was approved by the board of directors, enrollment has been implemented. This semester, the college will offer law courses, including a law department and a political economy department, as well as a local autonomy specialization course and a tax specialization course. Free Talk

A Piece of Insight

— Qiu Shui

Why does a woman close her eyes when she kisses a man? This question is easy to solve. It is because it is a natural instinct of human beings, like a doe hiding in the forest when it sees the tracks of a hunter, a kind of ridiculous behavior.

Ordinary women, on average, spend almost half their lives (closing their eyes) pretending not to know or see. Because she knows that if she tells men everything in her heart, men will no longer be attached to her.

If a woman clearly tells her man that she loves him, it will surely scare him or make him feel pain. If she tells him she doesn't love him, it will hurt his vanity and ruin his self-esteem. So she can only close her eyes and give people a riddle to guess.

In the world, only the future is most likely to move people's hearts, and only dreams are most likely to excite people's interest. A riddle can make people go through fire and water without hesitation. The reason why women can bewitch all living beings lies only in this move.

Being afraid of one's wife is not a virtue for men, and at the same time, it will definitely not win the favor of women. Because most women will never love a man who is willing to be submissive, and what women hope for is to have a brave and decisive protector.

Love is sacred, but sin often occurs in love. The source of this sin is because people cannot understand sacred love.

Radio Telephone in Hu Hanmin's Residence

— Li Qingduo

In recent years, science has flourished. Wireless telephones have become a very common means of communication. Those who are thousands of miles apart and need many days to travel by boat and car can communicate with each other in a few tens of minutes, which can be said to be very convenient. Many foreigners use wireless telephones. In the United States, it is said that nearly six or seven out of ten households use them, which shows its prevalence. Mr. Hu Zhantang, Speaker of the National Government's Legislative Yuan, installed a wireless telephone in his private residence in the capital in order to stay informed. The machine cost more than 200 gold, and the style is new and the sound is clear. Mr. Hu listens to all kinds of airwaves on the radio telephone in his spare time. He can listen to everything at will, such as the speeches of important people in the capital or the singing of the Little Luzon Opera Troupe. When the wireless telephone broadcasts, he can hear everything clearly. Therefore, although Mr. Hu is busy with official business every day, he has this kind of entertainment at home for recreation in his spare time. His spirit is very happy, and the news is extremely sensitive. It is reported that the Ministry of Finance has recently ordered that this item be exempt from import and export duties in order to encourage the use of this kind of wireless telephone at home.

Westernized Xi Zi

— He Haisheng, sent from Hangzhou

Recently, most of our country's women have short hair, long stockings, leather shoes, and cheongsams, tending towards Westernization. Their posture is graceful and moving. As for our Hangzhou's West Lake, it has always been known for its lake and mountain scenery. In the past, Resident Dongpo had a poem saying, "If you compare West Lake to Xi Zi, it is always suitable whether lightly dressed or heavily made up." Therefore, West Lake is also known as Xi Zi Lake. Rich people leisurely wander among them, so Western-style houses stand in rows, and roads are built, bridges are transformed, and so on. West Lake is also gradually becoming Westernized.

A few days ago, Director of Public Works Zhu Yaoting demolished the stone tablet at Broken Bridge Remnant Snow to facilitate traffic. One of the Ten Scenes of West Lake is missing. Recently, Mayor Cai Zengji has also made many plans for the construction of West Lake, completing the asphalt roads around the lake, building public halls in four places: Three Pools Mirroring the Moon, Autumn Moon over the Calm Lake, Ruangong Mound, and Lake Heart Pavilion, installing lights around the lake, building the Ge Ling Observatory, building boat wharves and docks, and adding gasoline machine ferries to save time for sightseeing. Guidance and reception centers for lake tours have been established. All construction projects use scientific methods and are created with artificial art. The Bureau of Public Works has been ordered to design and implement the projects so that the scenery of West Lake can be comparable to that of Europe and the United States. From then on, the natural beauty of Xi Zi Lake will be entirely transformed into a new trend and become a Westernized beauty. At the time of women with short, fluffy hair and leather shoes, those who come to visit Xi Zi Lake are no different from competing with Xi Zi in beauty. A smile. (Returned with thanks)

Folk Customs of Leping

— Zheng Yimei

Leping County belongs to the Xunyang Circuit of Jiangxi. The folk customs are savage, no different from outside the realm of civilization. There must be one or two armed fights every year. During the armed fights, hundreds or thousands of people often gather in the square, each holding knives and sticks, fighting bravely. If there are deaths or injuries, the blood-stained clothes are hung in the ancestral hall as a memorial. During the spring and autumn sacrifices, each side silently swears against the blood-stained clothes, regarding the other as an irreconcilable enemy, and the armed fight begins. Once there is an armed fight, the blood-stained clothes are added, so they are densely hung all over the ancestral hall. The bloody atmosphere is pungent and unbearable to see, and the feud becomes deeper and deeper, and there is no day to resolve it. A certain gentleman felt pity for them and thought that the blood-stained clothes were shocking to the eye and were the beginning of quarrels. He plotted to burn them to calm the people and no longer see the tragedy of severed necks and broken limbs. However, the plot was leaked and heard by the leader of the armed fight, who immediately built a high platform in the square and forced the gentleman to sit on it. After he ascended the seat, he removed the ladder and then made his followers bow down below, ostensibly to express their gratitude for his virtue, but secretly cutting off his food and drink, exposing him to the sun and rain, and wanting to kill him. Sure enough, he died in less than three days. Although the authorities knew about it, there was nothing they could do. This is a recent event, told by a Gan friend who came to avoid the Communist bandits.

What I Know About the Anhui Bandit Three-Legged

— Junmei

I read the article "Three-Legged, the Bandit Leader of Guangde" written by Wenxia in the 30th issue of this journal. The description of his deeds is very detailed. When I lived in She County in the past, I knew his deeds very well, so I wrote them in Free Talk to tell the truth.

Three-Legged originally had no great name. He was from She County. His surname was Wang. His ancestors were extremely noble, but by the time of Three-Legged, his family had declined, and he was no longer as heroic as he used to be. Three-Legged was born with a strange personality. He liked to walk in narrow alleys. When he was studying in a private school, he could support himself on the narrow walls with both hands and two feet and climb to the top of the house. His peers all admired his skills. When he grew up, he learned the tea business. Anhui tea leaves are usually sold with tung oil. The distance from the stack to the shop may be more than a mile, so the apprentices who are hired must be strong and powerful to be responsible for the transportation. For others, each bucket of tung oil must be transported by two people, but not for Three-Legged. He carries it on his shoulder and walks as usual. He usually wears iron sheets between his knees and ankles as usual. Over time, he can walk very fast. Once he removes the iron sheets, he can travel a hundred miles in an instant. This is the origin of the name Three-Legged. However, since Three-Legged started his business, he still did not reduce his old habit of walking diagonally in narrow alleys. He was repeatedly reprimanded by the manager and left the store in anger. At that time, bandits in Anhui were rising, and the people held self-defense groups. Because of this, Three-Legged was able to join the Huining County self-defense group and serve as a police officer. He learned the skills of the divine painter there. However, since then, She County has never seen his踪跡 again. At first, he did not expect that he would fall into the hands of bandits. I have not returned to my hometown since I went to Anhui five years ago because of something. Fish and geese are mostly misunderstood by Hong Qiao, and wandering sons often miss their hometown. Recently, home reports say that bandits are rampant everywhere. Reading Xiajun's article, I can't help but feel sad. With Three-Legged's body and unique skills, he should have followed the right path but did not, but harmed the villages and towns, which is really a pity.

A Tragic Incident in a Melon Field

— Yan Ye

Villagers often build sheds with supports and curtains in their melon fields to guard against theft, calling them melon sheds, where they sleep day and night. This year, a tragic incident occurred in a melon shed in Cibei, Zhejiang, involving a ferocious beast devouring a person, which is so extraordinary and horrifying that it is recorded here.

In Cibei, there was a farmer named Zhang, who grew melons every year as a side income. This year, he planted three mu of watermelons, and the harvest was abundant. Although he worked hard day and night, sleeping in the melon field and carrying melons to the market, he did not feel it was too difficult. One day last month, Zhang carried melons to the market, expecting to be gone overnight. Before leaving, he entrusted his wife with the responsibility of guarding the melon field at night. It is common for a wife to take over when her husband is away. Zhang had only one wife and one son, who was not yet ten years old. In the evening, the wife locked the door and took her son to the melon field. Under the bright stars and moon and the gentle evening breeze, the mother and son chatted happily, finding it enjoyable. After a while, the child grew tired and fell into a deep sleep. The mother felt lonely and also fell asleep. Later that night, the bed suddenly shook, and the mother woke up in fright. Through her sleepy eyes, she saw a ferocious beast climbing onto the bed. Terrified, she wanted to scream, but her son's cries of agony revealed that he had already been snatched away. The mother was extremely anxious and screamed as she gave chase. However, the beast moved quickly and was soon out of reach. In the darkness, she could only hear her son's agonizing cries. She continued to follow the sound, but soon it fell silent. She stood there and wailed loudly. In the vast wilderness at night, who could come to her aid? Feeling helpless, she rushed back home and woke up the neighbors, telling them what had happened. Dozens of strong men, carrying lamps and weapons, followed the mother in pursuit. They searched tirelessly, but to no avail. The commotion continued throughout the night, but it was all in vain. As dawn approached, they suddenly saw splashes of blood on the boundary. The crowd followed the blood forward, and the blood led them to a grove of trees. There was even more blood there, and they found two white bones. Deeper in the forest, they discovered a head. The mother looked down and recognized the familiar features. It was indeed her son. She picked up the head and wailed in grief, nearly fainting. The crowd quickly helped the mother, carried the head, and returned home together. They hurried to the market to tell Zhang what had happened. Zhang's grief was even greater than his wife's, as he was over fifty years old, and this son was born to him in his later years. His wife was also past childbearing age, and he felt even more pitiful for his future.

— Compiled by Tian Xu Wo Sheng

Recently, reports have surfaced about people in Shanghai being injured by strong acid thrown at their faces. In fact, there are three types of strong acid, which are strong acids. "Invincible Brand" toothpaste uses magnesium carbonate as its main ingredient. To prove this, if you put strong acid in a glass and pour in toothpaste, it will immediately turn into Dutch water and lose its corrosive properties. Therefore, if strong acid splashes onto the skin, do not wipe it with water, as this will only spread the damage. Instead, quickly pour "Invincible Brand" toothpaste onto it, and the strong acid will be absorbed and neutralized. Then, wash it off with water and apply more toothpaste. This will not only immediately relieve the pain but also prevent scarring. If you wipe it with your hands or a handkerchief first, the skin will become uneven and scarred after healing.

Strong acids such as hydrochloric acid, acetic acid, and oxalic acid can be fatal if swallowed. However, if you quickly mix "Invincible Brand" toothpaste with water to form a milky liquid and administer it to the person, the magnesium hydroxide will immediately neutralize the strong acid wherever it reaches, effectively turning danger into safety. "Invincible Brand" stomach medicine is especially effective, as it is made with magnesium oxide, and one dose is equivalent to three doses of other medications.

For skin burns caused by caustic soda, caustic potash, or ammonia, wash with boric acid or citric acid solution. Then, apply "Invincible Brand" type B frostbite ointment.

For burns caused by hot water or fire, apply "Invincible Brand" butterfly cream for good results. Alternatively, mix "Invincible Brand" toothpaste with Westin oil or hair cream and apply it to relieve pain and reduce swelling, preventing suppuration.

For any type of boil or sore that does not heal for a long time, apply a small amount of "Invincible Brand" toothpaste, and it will scab over and heal overnight.

The Roman Catholic Church's Dissent Regarding Chinese Customs (Part 1)

— Li Liu Zeng, sent from Paris

According to a recent dispatch from Rome published in the Paris Times, the Holy Office of the Vatican has reaffirmed its 1710 ruling prohibiting discussions on whether the Catholic Church can permit Chinese people to honor Confucius and their ancestors. The ruling claims that these customs are merely disguised idol worship.

The issue involved in this dispatch has a long history. Two hundred years ago, Catholics in China were already engaged in fierce disputes over this matter, causing a great sensation. Now that the old issue has been brought up again, it is feared that it will inevitably cause many more disputes. There are many writings discussing this issue, and the process is quite interesting.

The Jesuit order first established itself in China in the mid-16th century. From that time on, it was the fierce rival of the Dominican order. It is well known that these two orders represent two opposing tendencies within the Catholic Church. The Jesuit order emphasizes spirituality and neglects dogma, while the Dominican order believes that everything is false except for the Bible. The conflict between the two orders began with a dispute over a sacred book in the Spanish religious court. Therefore, it was expected that there would be fierce disturbances in China. In 1633, the Spanish Dominican order, jealous of the success of the Jesuit order in spreading religion in China, also launched a large-scale eastward expansion. After arriving in China, they claimed that the emperors and sages of China were suffering in hell, and the Qing court issued a ban, ordering them to stop such preaching or be immediately expelled.

Having gained the upper hand in China, the Dominican order became increasingly angry with the Jesuit order, criticizing them for allowing Chinese believers to continue worshiping their ancestors and Confucius, thereby preserving their original superstitions. On September 12, 1645, Pope Innocent X, at the request of the Dominican order, issued an edict prohibiting Chinese Catholics from performing any rituals for the dead. However, the Jesuit order did not comply with the edict. On March 23, 1656, Pope Alexander VII ordered the Jesuit order to explain why they were allowing the Chinese to worship their ancestors.

The open and secret struggles between the two orders continued until the early years of the Kangxi reign. At that time, the southeastern provinces often reported illegal activities by the Spanish Dominican order. The Qing court issued an order on January 4, 1665, prohibiting all Catholic preaching. Missionaries were placed under surveillance.

Warmth in My Heart (269)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Green Bamboo Tears Stain Her Heart, Red Lotus Fragrance Fades as a Maiden's Soul Departs

Cuiyun had bought her freedom, and her body was finally free. However, she was now under economic pressure. That particular customer wanted her to continue her life as a prostitute. It was like a freed serf who had to establish his own business and support his family, or like a newly independent country that had to prepare for all kinds of construction. Money was essential. However, if you needed money immediately, the creditor groups in the brothel world were already circling around you. However, they had very strict conditions and very high interest rates. Cuiyun was a timid person and did not dare to take on too much debt. However, if you wanted to start a new chapter, running things independently, renting a room, and trying to make a name for yourself, you couldn't be worse off than before. Before, you were a colony, a protected state. Now that you were independent, you had to put on a show so you wouldn't be laughed at. That meant you had to pay attention to detail, and in order to satisfy this desire to win, you couldn't help but borrow a little more money. Moreover, in that kind of society, it was a snobbish society. They said, "If you don't spend small money, you won't make big money." If your room was well-decorated, fully equipped, and everything you used was of the highest quality, you would naturally attract higher-class customers. Second-class customers would often be intimidated by your grandeur and retreat, knowing their limits. If you had a downstairs room that was not fully equipped, with no stove in the winter and no fan in the summer, and customers came to drink and play mahjong but you didn't have anything, with bums always standing at the door, the customers would frown when they stepped inside, feeling that they would lose face inviting guests to such a place. So, you would attract a group of customers who were just barely acceptable, and there would often be brawls and damage to the room. Both the host and the guests would be embarrassed. Higher-class customers would never do such things. As the saying goes, "If you want to do a good job, you must first sharpen your tools." This is true in all things, and a brothel is no exception. The price of Cuiyun's independence was seven or eight hundred yuan. If Huayunting had paid that seven or eight hundred yuan, she could have paid off the principal and interest. When she first opened her room, her business was not bad. Although she couldn't squeeze into the ranks of top-tier celebrities in the flower world, she could be considered a second-tier celebrity. At that time, the society of courtesans was divided into literary and military factions. The military faction was flamboyant, liked to argue and make noise, and their attire was deliberately strange. The literary faction was quiet, good at socializing, and skilled in rhetoric. The military faction sang black-faced male roles and old male roles, while the literary faction sang Kunqu opera and Qingyi roles. However, at that time, the trend was gradually changing, with more emphasis on the military and less on the literary. Those girls who sang nonsense tunes, slept with actors and grooms, were liked by many customers. They couldn't talk to the quiet girls and found them boring. Therefore, you could observe the changes in the world in the brothel world.
